Capitol .xl.	 The end.

So autras apostemas les quals cove que sian traucatz quan son cruzes, e no son maturatz segon lor compliment, ayssi cum apostemas que son propdas a las juncturas, quar apostema quan ve prop junctura, lo esser de lu es prolonguat entro que·s poyreys aquo que es en le circuit de lu, e fort leu son corromputz les liamentz o les nervis de aquela junctura, per que es fayta causa de contraccio de aquel membre; o es apostema prop de membre principal, e si tu tardas la perforacio de lu entro sia madurat nosira al membre principal; o es prop le cul, donc perfora aque no-madurat; e no cove que·l perforas cru, de no-complida degestio, sino aquel que es prop del cul, per so que no poyresca le preon de lu e sia elonguat a las partidas dedintz del cul, e sia fayta fistula, o que sia fayt en le terme de lu que no sia sanat. E perforacio tostemps sia per le lonc de la carn o del cors, si las apostemas son en las partidas de las mas o dels pes, e en loc dels lacertz, de las cordas dels nervis, de las arcerias; e, al derier, en totz locs enguals en les quals no es reflecio; quar en aquels que so reflectitz, usa de perforacio segon aquel membre. Don guarda aquest capitol am gran cautela, e aprop la tua perforacio en la qual perforas aquestz apostemas, cove que abstergescas las plagues e consideras donc si la plagua del apostema es pauca, o es una seccio plana, lahoras tu aministra las qualguas de li o de coto antic; e si le apostema es gran, e las fissuras de la perforacio son motas, lahoras cove que tu pauses meca en quascun trauc entro que pervenguan ensemps. E si en le apostema es abscindit una partida de la codena o has concavada aquela en le circuit, lahoras cove que tu la complescas de coto viel o de fil fayt de drap de li, ayssi cum quan has traytz pans o razizos, ses humiditat; e strenh aquel entro al tertz dia; e aprop proceseys aquel e cura le am aquo que cove dels enguentz entro que sia sanat.	 If the incision is completely closed or convexly curved, then you must apply a dressing to it and wait until morning; if there are any tears or fissures in addition to them, keep them moist, and stretch that part every third day; take care of this and cure whatever comes into contact with it so that everything becomes healthy.

Capitol .xli.	 The sixty-first chapter.
De seccio de apostemas les quals veno en la codena del cap.	 In the following section, we will examine those that appear in the scalp area.
En la codena del cap petitz apostemas, e so de specias de nodes les quals conteno tunicas que so a lor factz ; e las specias de lor so motas.	 In the scalp region, there are two types of nodules that contain tunics which can be seen; and the smaller ones.
E de lor son pingas, e de aquelas so que conteno humiditat semblant a lima.	 The nodules on them are small, and those containing moisture similar to lime.
E de aquelas so las quals conteno humiditat semblant a pols, et asemblantz a lor; e de aquelas so que son lapideas, durs.	 The nodules of the latter type contain moisture similar to dust, and they are rough on the outside; and those that are soft.
E en la seccio de totz, e en la extraccio de aquels no es temor, cum deves la exteccio de aquels no fa contrariat arceria.	 In all sections, except in the section dealing with them [nodules], and apart from their removal there is no need to worry; but when it comes time for removing these, then you should not let your guard down.

The edges of the incision should be sharp and the others smooth or rounded, not to cause any damage to blood vessels or nerves, for those reasons the surgeon aims to minimize pain in the patient's body and provide a comfortable environment during the healing process after the operation.

The areas that are affected by these humors tend to be the joints and extremities (hands, feet), which may cause pain due to their sensitivity and lack of protection in cold conditions, hence it is not considered medical treatment when experienced at the first onset.

Stomachache from a blockage in the umbilical vein or artery (due to a tear), constipation causing intestinal obstruction, or from a narrowed section of the intestine itself.

Mays si per humiditat, lahoras es leon e no es occultat quan premes am la tua ma, ni es constrengut, ni es cregut.	 The pain may be due to moisture (inflammation), but it won't stop if you press on the area with your hand or feel for anything inside; there is no feeling of constriction or fullness.

If the abscess is located in the groin region or in the abdominal wall, doctors instruct the patient to keep it intact as much as possible, and extend their arm over that area towards the other side of their body so they can monitor for any signs of leakage, also instructing them to gently press on the abdomen to feel if there are any contractions.

If you miss the abscess and it doesn't leak, doctors instruct to squeeze as hard as possible to try to get rid of it and urge them to press firmly on their abdomen to feel for any contractions that may indicate leakage.

De curacio de cranc.	 About care for a wound
Ja havem dit, en la divisio, de specia de cranc e en qual manieyra es via a la curacio de lu am medicinas, e que es squivador en lu la curacio am ferr per so que no sia ulcerat; e havem dit cranc engendrat en la mayra e cautela de la curacio de lu.	 We have said that in the division of care for a wound and how to approach it from medical practices, which is important when carrying out such care because not all wounds are ulcers; we have also mentioned the generation of new wounds through excessive caution in caring for them.
E diyssero les antics que alcunas veguadas cranc es en loc on es possibla la eradicacio de lu, ayssi cum de cran le qual es en las mamillas o en la coyssa e a lor semblantz dels membres allocat a estrayre tot aquel, e majorment quan es comensant petit.	 Whenever old wounds are found in locations where it is possible to eradicate them, as well as when they appear on the breasts or buttocks and any other part of the body that can be reached with ease, especially if they occur first thing in the morning
Mays quan es antiquat e es gra, no cove que te propries a lu, quar yeu non pogui sanar de aquel alcu ni no he vist autre, ni que sia pervengut ad aquo.	 If it is old and large, do not attempt to remove it, because if you cannot heal from this wound or prevent further damage, do nothing about it.
E la operacio en lu es quan es allocat ayssi cum havem dit, es que tu precedescas e laysses le malaute e purgues de colera negra alcunas veguadas, e aprop sagna aquel, si es atrobada replecio manifesta.	 The operation is when it is inserted like this as we have said, you precede and loosen the ulcerated flesh with cold water jets some vegetables, and then proceed to that place if found clearly manifested.
E aprop prepara le malaute am preparacio en le qual sia locat am operacio, e aprop prohiceys en le trauc uncis les quals cove ad aquel; e aprop concava de tota part am la codena sego bona perexcrutacio entro que no romangua alcuna causa de las razitz de lu.	 Then prepare the ulcerated flesh for the operation, and proceed to that place where you were previously directed; then focus on a thorough examination of all parts until nothing remains unexplained in the causes of this disease.
E layssa correr le sanc, e no abscidas aquel leugierament, e exprem les locs, e abstergeys le sanc gros tot am la tua ma o am instrument am le qual es a tu possible dels instruments.	 Then loosen the sutures and remove them gradually, examine all places, and treat with the largest possible ointment or instrument that may be among your instruments.
Mays si a tu fa contrarietat de sanc gros inscizio de vena o de arceria, lahoras cauterisa aquela entro que·l flux del sanc sia cessat, e aprop cura aquel am l’autra curacio entro que sia sanat.	 If it is necessary to make incisions of vein or artery, the ulcers will be burned until the flow of blood has ceased, and then treat as before with another treatment.

De castracio.	 Castration.
Sapias que castratio en nostre ley es excomengada, mays per causa es legut a mi que·m remembre de lu en aquest libre; e no es necessaria la rememoracio de lu sino per doas manieyras, de las quals es la una per so que aquo sia en la sciensa del metge quan es enterroguat de aquela, que sapia la curacio de lu al qual accideys; e l’autra manieyra es que nos motas vetz havem necessitat de castracio de autras bestias per les juvamentz nostres per aquelas, ayssi cum de motos, e de bocs, e de porcs, e de semblantz a las bestias. E donc dic que castracio es fayta en dos manieyras: o per atrissio, o per fissura a seccio.	 Castration occurs in two manners: either by traction or through a cut
Mays en aquela que es fayta per atrissio, la via de la opera es que nos fassam cezer la bestia en aygua cauda entro que·ls genetius de lu sian mollificatz e sian linhitz e que pendan.	 When castrated by traction, the method of operation is to cut off the foreskin inside so that both testicles are softened and lined up, and they hang down.
E aprop pren aquels am la tua ma entro que sian resols e no apparescan dejos le tocament.	 The approach taken here is to remove it gently without making any cuts.
Mays en castracio fayta per fissura e seccio, cove que tu tenguas la bestia e premas la codena dels testicols de lu am la ma senestra.	 When castrated by cutting and tearing, you will have the penis held in place between the testicles of the patient with a hand on either side.
E aprop lia le suspensori, e inscideys sobre quascun huou am una seccio entro que dos huous proceseysso.	 The suspenders are tightened and incisions made to ensure that both tubes remain separate
E aprop inscideys aquels pus que auras quascu excorjat.	 When castrated, the incision is made below the scrotum.
E no leysses sobre aquels del ciphac alcuna causa, sino le ciphac subtil le qual es sobre les vazes.	 Nothing else is mentioned except for the use of a catheter which is placed in the urethra.
E aquesta manieyra de castracio es milhor la qual es fayta per atrissio, quar atrissio fort leu layssa alcuna causa dels testicols per que la bestia desira coyt.	 The method of castration through traction is superior to that done through cutting and tearing as the foreskin can still cause harm to the testicles if it becomes detached.
E aprop cura la plagua entro que sia sanada.	 After surgery, care must be taken so that the wound heals properly.

E si vols cauteriza la formiga segon que es denant dit en la cauterizacio de atheyl en le capitol de cauteri.	 "If you wish to cauterize the ulcer in the same way as for arteries, then cauterize it at the tip of a cautery.
De forma dels instrumentz que so aministratz a dar cristeri.	 "From among the instruments that are used by doctors:
Alcunas veguadas es fayt cristeri de argent o de lato o de eram fondut o malleat; e alcunas veguadas es fayt de aquels instrumentz petit e gran segon aquels als quals so aministratz, quar aquel que es aministrat en la curacio dels petitz enfants sia petit; e de aquel dels quals los culs son freuls o doloyrozes, les cristeris de aquels sian petitz. La forma de cristeri gran e pauc:	 "The form of large ones (large cauteries):
Le cap de la canula de lu desus en le qual es liada la borsa sia ampla segon aquesta manieyra; e sia a lu distinacio la on la borsa es liada ayssi cum vezes.	 "The top of the needle's point, where you will place a bag wide enough in this manner.
E la extremitat de lu pus dejus, la qual es entromesa en le cul, sia sorda (so es no-uberta) mot leon, atrasent a subtilita; e en la un del latz de lu sian dos traucs, e en l’autre costat un trauc, e sia la amplesa del trauc segon la groseza dels rays e pus gros un petit. E sia la borsa en la qual sian pausadas las medicinas de vesica de bestia o de pel de ovelha, e la razit de lu sia un palm.	 The bag in which the bladder medicines of beast or sheep are placed is dry and rough
E sia perforada per motz traucs ayssi cum es revolvuda; e si l’espazi le qual es entre les traucs la grossetut del dit.	 It is perforated by sharp ulcers, which turn it around like this; if there is space between the ulcers then its surface will be rough
E aprop entromet en aquels traucs fiel fort de fiel cru le qual sia de detz fiels, o enviro aquels; e ajusta am aquel la borsa; e quan es pausada en lu la borsa, sia streyt en le cap del cristeri entre dos distingentz am fort costriccio, e aprop cristeriza am aquel quascun trauc: Mays la qualitat de cristerizar am aquel es que tu omples la borsa de la medicina, que sia escalfada segon la quantitat de la tolleransa del malaute; e guarda te que no sia trop cauda ni trop freja. E si la medicina forsa aquel a eyssiment, tengua le tant quant poyra; e si dorm am aquel per tota una nueyt, es mays derier en juvament.	 When medicine fails to heal that illness completely, then it may be necessary in the future.

De curacio de las plaguas.	 For healing of the wounds.
Yeu ja e dit en la divisio de la curacio de las plaguas aquo que convenia al libre, e yeu dic assi la curacio de aquelas am ma e am medicinas segon le conpliment.	 You have already mentioned in the previous part of the healing process that it was customary to follow a free course for treatment, and you mention here that medical treatments should be based on this course as well.
Donc dic que las plaguas son diversificadas segon aquo en que son faytas las plaguas e segon le loc sobre le qual cazo las plaquas.	 Therefore, the wounds are classified according to whether they were caused by cold humors or other factors affecting their location.
E las causas per que motas vetz son faytas las plaguas so ayssi cum getament de peyra, o inscisio d’espaza o de cotel, o percussio am lansa, o am fustz, o am sageta, o semblantz ad aquels de motas causas. Mays las plaguas que so en les locz del cos so ayssi cum plagua la qual catz sobre le cap, o·l col, o·l pietz, o·l ventre, o·l fitge, e semblantz ad aquels dels membres. E yeu so recomtant la curacio de alcunas plaguas per que pauses aquela ratiocinacio e regla sobre las autras plaguas.	 This sentence translates to English as: You should apply some plaguings in order to prevent another reasoning and regulation of the subsequent plaguings.
E yeu comensare de las plaguas del cap simplas, quar la rememoracio de las compostas vindra al comensament del tertz capitol.	 This sentence translates to English as: You should start with simple plagues, and then recall the complex ones will begin at the third capital.
Donc dic que quan accideys en le cap plagua simpla e no es fractura, lahoras considera: si es per getament de peyra o de semblant, e ja ha trinquada la codena tant solament e es gran plagla e temes sobre aquel malaute havinement de apostema caut, lahoras tu te coyta e fleubotoma la cephalica tantost, e no tardas aquo; e extrats ad aquel del sanc segon la quantitat de la vertut de lu si no mes alcuna causa prohibent de fleubotomia, majorment si·l sanc que es eyssit de la plagua es pauc.	 This sentence translates to English as: When you encounter a simple plague that hasn't broken it, the doctor considers: if this is for healing or relief, and there has been no bloodletting associated with its application, then apply this potion gently; but if any bleeding occurs, quickly remove the cephalica (a type of poultice used to stop bleeding) from around it.
E sia la flaubotomia del contrari de la partida plaguada; e guardase le malaute de replecio e de vi e de viandas grossas.	 This sentence translates to English as: And be careful of the opposite of the diseased plague, and keep the patient away from large wounds and from any excessive bleeding.
Mays si de la minuicio prohibeys alcuna causa, lahoras sia aminorat de la vianda e no apropinque a carn ni a vi.	 This sentence translates to English as: If there is no prohibited cause, then the doctor should gently remove the wound and avoid applying it to skin or to blood.
E pausa sobre la plagua, si a lu accideys apostema caut, coto enfus en oli rozat solet o en vi en le qual es stipticat.	 This sentence translates to English as: Upon the plague, if bleeding occurs in or on it, mix oil and vinegar (or any other liquid) with a compress applied gently over it.
Mays si est segur de apostema caut, lahoras pausa sobre la plagua, si es recent am le sieu sanc e le ayre no ha mudat aquela la polvera la qual yeu recomtare aprop petit.	 This sentence translates to English as: If you are sure of bleeding, then upon the plague apply a compress if it is fresh and the wound has not changed much from what was recommended for application earlier.
E si le ayre ja ha mudada aquela, lahoras pausa sobre alscus enguentz entro que sia sanada.	 When the patient's belly has been made open, put down cushions on either side to keep it from falling in, while someone holds their hands.
Mays si la plagua es gran o es per inscizio d’espaza e de semblantz, e no so ajustadas las labias de lu per puvils, lahoras ajusta aquelas am sutura segon que yeu recomtare de la sutura de lor.	 If the wound is large or gaping and cannot be closed with stitches due to risk of infection, then doctors adjust it to close later after making a separate incision for sutures.
Mays si la plagua ja es discuberta del os e pen, e no es retencio de lu sino un petit suspensori, lahoras inscideys aquela e aprop cura la plagua am medicinas e restaura la carn aprop en loc de codena, e comanda al malaute que sia pescut de viandas en las quals es groceza: caps e formen coyt e semblantz a lor, entro que sia compost.	 If the belly wound is visible and gaping, then doctors insert something to keep it open until healing is complete, making an incision for sutures as well in order to close it later on in another place, so that the flesh is stitched up correctly there while preventing waste from accumulating: heads and forms should be straight and similar.
E si atrobas en la codena putrefaccio e no adhereys al os, lahoras tu inscideys tot aquo poyrit e geta aquo, e aprop cura aquo.	 If the belly wound becomes rotten or adheres to the abdomen, then doctors cut through it and remove it, treating the affected area as necessary.
Mays si en aquestas plaguas es arteria o vena de la qual fluxs de sanc pot evenir, e no es abscindida per medicinas, lahoras tu inquier sobre la arteria, e si atrobas aquela no-inscidida, lahoras tu inscideys aquela am spatum, o lia aquela; e si necessitat te provoca que aquo que havem dit no comfereys, lahoras tu cauteriza entro que·l sanc sia abscidit. E la manieyra de la polvera es aquesta: recipe oli de enses partida una, de sanc de drago partida doas, de caus no-extincta partidas tres; sia tot mot trissat e crivellat, e de lu sia la plagua omplida, e sia constrengida per bona constriccio entro que be sobre aquela aderesca, e sia coagulada am le sanc.	 The first sentence means: "The recipe for treating the patient's ailment is to apply a poultice once every day, and to change dressings three times; it should consist of linen well-padded with vinegar and strained cloth tightly bound around the afflicted part so that they do not loosen or separate from one another.
E aprop strengeys aquela desus am pulvils e leyssa aquela, e no la deslias mentre esta ayssi que no es apostemada, quar no es eredicada de lu la medicina entro que sia sanada. E alcuna vetz fa aquo sola cautz, quan no es a tu en present enses e sanc de drago.	 "It should not only involve applying poultices when there is also pain in the affected areas and legs.

E si le ayre las ha alteradas, e majorment quan es en temps d’estiu, lahoras no es entencio a la posicio de aquesta polvera, mays adonc cura aquelas am aquo que havem dit, enayssi que tu pauses sobre aquelas alcus enguents degistius, o que pauses sobre aquelas pols de la farina del ordi am aygua e mel entro que getan poyredura; e aprop cura aquelas am l’autra curacio entro que sian sanadas. E ventozacio no extratz le sanc sino de las venas menudas sparssas en la carn, e per aquo no catz la vertut per aquelas, ayssi cum es cazement per fleubotomia; ni no cove que ventozacio sia fayta am foc o ses foc en alcuna malautia fayta per replecio entro que le cors tot sia evacuat.	 The object does not extract flesh but only the veins in small parts of the flesh, and therefore it is done together with phlebotomia; nor that an incision be made at fire or flames under any circumstances to prevent the body from being evacuated.
Mays si necessitat provoca a ventozacio per malautia o per continua, aministrem aquela en tota hora al comensament del mes e en la fi de lu, e en le mieg loc de lu e en qualque temps sia.	 When there is a need to perform surgery for the patient either in the middle of the month or at the end of it, we will administer that treatment from every corner of the place and whenever necessary
La qual causa es quar dels homes es en les quals es sanc multiplicat entro que indigeys de extraccio de lu per ventozacio e atroba en le sieu cap graveza e soda; e de aquels es que atroba replecio e rogor en la sua cara e en le sieu cap, e en le sieu col; e de aquels es que atroba pruziment en la sua cara e en le sieu front e tenebrositat e hebetut en les sieus huels; e de aquels que gieta le loc de la sua ventozacio; e de aquels es que le lor ris es multiplicat; e de aquels es que atroba gustament de sanc en la sua boca, o que la lengua es apostemada e escup sanc; e de aquels es que lor dormir es multiplicat, e de aquels que vetz sanc en lo dormir rogor e antics e plaguas e autras causas a lor semblantz.	 These are the men who have inflicted wounds that extend to their skull and cause severe damage, or those who inflict wounds on their face and tongue causing pain when speaking, or those who multiply sores in their sleep, or those whose sleep is multiplied leading to nightmares.
E donc quan vezes en alcuna causa de aquelas, e propriament si es en le tertz o miga del mes, lahoras comandam ventozacio esser fayta pus que so passadas del dia dos o tres horas.	 And when it comes to any of these cases, and especially if it is at the third or middle of the month, the doctors order that surgery be performed within three or two hours.
E juvament de ventozacio de la nuca es que quan aquela confereys a gravitat en le cap e ad aquo que es efondit als huels; mays cove que aquo sia aprop evacuacio de tot le cors.	 The first sentence should be translated as: "The doctors order that the treatment of surgery for that particular case is to occur as soon as possible, and it is necessary that the cause of this severity in the head must also bring about a complete evacuation from every part of the body.
E aquesta ventoza es en le loc de fleubotomia de la cephalica.	 The first sentence should be translated as: "The treatment for surgery performed due to cephalic phlebotomy is at the site where it occurs.
E no es legut que use de lu aquel que es de frega complecio, o en le qual es catarr, quar dona ad aquel gran nocument.	 When complex bleeding occurs or when there is a great abundance of phlegm in that part, it can lead to great discomfort
E per aquo no cove que uso de aquela les vielhs, e en les caps dels quals so malautias frejas.	 You should not use those vessels if they are clogged or the veins where swelling occurs
Mays ad aquel que sobre aquela es continuant sobre lu es fayta oblivio; e per aquo cove que tu comandes al ventozador que depause la sua ma un petit am la ventosa a las partidas dejos, temen de la generacio de oblivio.	 When you continue to cover the affected part with your hand while it is still painful and when you want to prevent a recurrence of gout, ask the phlebotomist to pause for a moment by placing a small bandage over the area where pain occurs
Mays ventozacio de alkehel es en loc de fleubotomia de la vena fusca e de la basilica: e per aquo confereys a asma, e a la constriccio de ale e a la scissura del sturment de ale, e a tos, e a replecio.	 When the phlebotomist is in the location of the femoral artery and the basilic vein, they will confirm that there are no obstructions or narrowing of the arteries or veins, which means the procedure can be safely performed
E cove que sia enpellida la ventoza alkehel un petit, quar si es pausada dejos, engendra debilitat en le cors e en le stomac.	 When you place a small bandage on the affected area and pause it if it is done, there will be weakness in the body or stomach
E la ventozacio de alhagdahan confereys a las dolors accident en le cap e a obtalmia, e emigranea, e prefocacio, e a dolors en las razitz de las dentz; e es en loc de fleubotomia de la basiliqua.	 The phlebotomist will confirm the presence of any discomfort in the head, sight, voice, and pain in the teeth or gums, as well as in the location of the basilic vein.
E cove que comandes al ventozador que no prema la sua ma am scarificacio per que no inscida la arteria e accida fluxs de sanc.	 Ask the phlebotomist to avoid making any small incisions that may cause bleeding in the artery and restrict blood flow.
E ventozacio dejos le mento comfereys a alcola en la boca, e a corrupcio de la gingiva, e a semblantz a lor de las malautias que so en la boca, e stan en loc de fleubotomia de aliheric que so en las doas labias.	 The phlebotomist will check the mouth for any ulcers or gum infections that may be present and in the location of the basilic vein on both sides of the neck.
Mays la ventozacio que es fayta sobre las doas spatulas confereys a caphatan, le qual es fayt per replecio de caliditat.	 When joint pain is caused by cold humors that infiltrate each part of the body, and when there is pain in the feet, it is customary for doctors to call it gout.
E la ventosacio de las doas partidas dedintz dels focils confereys juvament de la fleubotomia de tres venas, so es de la basilica, fusca e cephalica, quar aquela atratz le sanc de totas aquelas venas pus manudas que so en la carn, e aquelas venas menudas de las autras venas pus grossas entro que pervengua la atraccio a las tres venas.	 The veins of the two feet, when inflamed by phlebotomy of three veins, are called basilica veins, and fusca, cephalica; because those arteries that are in the flesh, and those veins small among the larger ones that come out through the opening in the three veins.
E comanda al ventozador que trop no procezesca en scarificacio, quar le loc es denudat de carn, e dejos lu so nervis e arterias.	 The phlebotomist is commanded not to proceed with cutting, because it will damage the flesh and arteries.
E es una ventoza am la qual es ventozat sobre alshosses e confereys a las emorroydas del cul e a las ulceracios pus dejos.	 It is a treatment that involves applying it to the thighs, and also to the hemorrhoids of the anus and ulcers.
E cove que comandes al ventozador que sia gran ventoza, e que sia de eram, quar le loc indigeys de fort seccio; e fort leu so traucadas ventozas subtils e sia scarificat am scarificacio.	 The phlebotomist is commanded to make a large incision and also to make the small ones because the location requires fine dissection; and very thick incisions are not suitable for this procedure.
Mays ventozas de las cambas minueysso per minuicio manifesta, quar atiran le sanc de tot le cors, e comfereysso a dolors antiquas dels ronhos e de la mayre, e de la vesica; e provocan las mestruas, e comfereysso a bothor e ademil; e stan en loc de fleubotomia de doas sophenas, e alahorcoben, e de doas cavilhas.	 The veins of the legs are exposed in detail for inspection, and cause pain from the kidneys and bladder, as well as menstruation, and discomforts to both sexes; and there is phlebotomy on two feet, and also the two calves.
Enpero mot debelitan tot le cors e fan accidir sincopi en motz homes.	 "In one breath, throughout the chest, let's spread it evenly over each part of the body.
E de las ventozas alahorcoben le juvament es propda al juvament a las ventozas de doas cambas.	 "From the top to the bottom, move both legs at once towards the back of two steps.
E la qualitat de la posicio de las ventozas es que pauses la ventoza al comensament vueda e sucguas per succio temprada, e no prolongues la posicio de las ventozas, mays pausa aquelas leugierament, e reman aquelas coytadament, e que las humors venguan al loc per adveniment engual. E no cesses iterar aquo e continuar entro que veja le loc ja enrojezir e inflar e que appara la rogor del sanc.	 "Do not stop repeating this and continue until you see the redness appear and inflation, as well as when the question comes.
E lahoras tu scarifiqua e itera la succio pauc a pauc, e aprop considera en la dispozicio dels cors.	 "The pain will decrease little by little, and carefully consider each time you breathe in deeply.
Quar aquel home que es de tendra carn de rars pors, cove que tu le scarifiques una veguada e no pus, per que le loc no sia ulcerat.	 "For someone who has a rough skin surface like sandpaper, you should apply it sparingly and not rub too vigorously to prevent the area from being irritated.
E comanda al ventozador que amplifique la scarificacio e pronde un pauc, e atempre la succio am facilitat.	 "Instruct the masseur or physiotherapist gently massage in small amounts while breathing evenly.
E si en le sanc es grossitut, lahoras cove que scarifiques doas veguadas, quar en la primieyra veguada es uberta la via de subtiliacio al sanc e a la aquositat de lu.	 "If the pain is severe, apply two compresses at once, with one being very gentle in its approach and touchiness to the area.
Mays en la segunda a la perscrutacio aquisida de la extraccio del sanc gros.	 "In the second compress be cautious about avoiding any extra pressure on the affected area that is sensitive or prone to injury.
E si le sanc es mot feculent, lahoras sia fayta scarificacio la tersa veguada per que consiegua le derier.	 When there's a foul smell from the patient, the physicians will make an incision in order to reach the affected area and cure it
E derierament, quan volem extrayre le sanc pauc a pauc o un petit, abasta a nos una scarificacio.	 And if we want to remove only a little bit or just a small part of the foul smell, then we make an incision in that area.
E si volem extraccio de mot sanc, scarificam am mota scarificacio; e si nos conoyssem que·l sanc es gros, lahoras cove que scarifiquem per scarificacio preonda.	 And if we want to remove the foul smell completely and/or if it is necessary for the foul smell to be larger, then doctors make a more extensive incision.
E le terme de scarificacio en la qual es la profunditat de la codena tant solament.	 The depth of the incision depends on its purpose.
E si aquel del qual la codena es grossa, dura, fusca, e les sieus pors so streytz, cove que les locs de las ventosas sian untatz lenitius, apertius resolutius; si es en temps d’estiu, ayssi cum es oli de aloen o oli de violat, o oli de amellas dossas, o oli de cemensa de coja; e si es en temps ivern, lahoras oli narci, o oli de liri, o oli de camamilla, o de sanc, e ad aquels semblantz.	 If the abscess is large and filled with pus that causes difficulty in exuding, then it may be necessary to make an incision through which air can pass out easily so as to release pus more quickly; if done during summer, one may apply oil of lavender or violet or chamomile, or the same thing mentioned earlier.
E si la superfluitat es grossa, freja, lahoras le oli sia amaranti, o oli de balsamita, o oli de aloen, o oli aneti, e a lor semblantz. E aquel del qual le sanc es de mota humiditat, lava las suas ventozas am vi agre, o am aygua de mirt e sumac e semblant ad aquels.	 When someone has a runny nose that is due to moisture, blow their nostrils gently or with warm air, or with water from mist and salt or similar things
E de aquel del qual las superfluitatz son grossas, lava las suas ventozas am vi antic, o am aygua de sansuc, que es majorana, o de decoccio de anet, o de camamilla, e a lor semblantz. E cove que la ventozacio sia guardada denant de banh; habantz cove que sia aministrada aprop issiment del banh per una hora o per doas, e cove que dorma aprop la ventozacio.	 If the nose is blocked up, you should blow it gently and administer a decongestant in the form of a spray or drops every hour or two, and make sure to rest your nasal passages properly.
Quid est quo oportet ut regatur ventosandus aus phlebotomatus ante ventosationem.	 What is necessary to regulate blood flow in the nostrils before using nose drops?
Cove que consideras al comensament: lahoras si le ventozador o aquel que·s deu fleubotomar es coleric e ventz sobre lu sanc agut e imflamacio, lahoras cove que prengua causas infrigidantz, ayssi cum milgranas acetosas, e endivia an vi agre e laytuguas, e secanabin, e julep, e a lor semblantz. E pausa a lor viandas ayssi cum poletz, e carns de auzels serbiges, e viandas conditas am agras, e a lu semblantz.	 Take breaks in between doses, eat foods that are cold, such as those containing caffeine or alcohol, and drink fluids that have been cooked to kill bacteria, and similarly

When the complexion is affected by dryness, it's necessary to drink water or foods that contain caffeine and alcohol in moderation, take breaks from eating spicy and hot foods, avoid cold drinks like coffee and tea, and ensure you have enough to eat and drink, and pause the consumption of beverages containing caffeine or alcohol.
E cove que en lo dia de ventozacio e de fleubotomia le beure sia major que la vianda.	 When it's cold outside or when someone has a fever, drink more than water.
E cove que sia donat en beure en alcunas horas ad alcus homes tyriaca alpharac, o medicamentz de musc, so es muscada, o alcelita denant la ventozacio o denant fleubotomia o aprop, per so que·ls membres principals sian confortatz e que·l sanc sia subtiliat; e no cove que prenguan aquela scalfatz.	 If someone is given medication for a fever or cold and they are shivering or their main members are being affected by the cold outside or by fever, then these main parts should be warmed up gently so that they become comfortable and this prevents the skin from becoming too sensitive; do not give them anything else.
Mays las ventozas que so ses scarificacio sian ventozas que so pausadas sus le fetge, e sobre la melsa e podagra, e sobre le umbelic, en les locs dels jonolhs, e la pixida del ancha, quar aquestz membres no suffertan scarificacio sobre si.	 When the fingers are cold and stiff or if they become numb from being in a cool environment, over the hand, elbow and thumb joints, these parts should be rubbed gently so that they do not suffer from stiffness; do not rub them too much as it may cause harm to their structure.
E no es querit per aquelas sino atraccio de sanc de membre, ayssi cum pausam ventosa sobre mamilha en malautia de flux de sanc del sanc de las nars; e usam de aquela per que sia dissolvuda ventositat freja inviscade del membre, ayssi cum pausam sobre le ventre e l’umbelic; quar aquela rarifique le membre e scalfa lu e ramau la dolor quar resolveys ventositat.	 It is not advisable to do this because if the numbness occurs in the fingers and reaches up to the elbow or the thumb joint, then it may cause harm to these parts of the body; also it will dissolve coldness that enters through the nose and reach down into the member, over the belly and the elbow, causing that part of the member to be stiffened and scalped, making pain worse as it resolves the cold.
E ja es pausada sobre les ronhos quan accideys en lor opilacio o poyra, quar per vertut de atraccio fort leu huobre opilacio e erradica le poyra de son loc.	 When you sneeze or cough, it is advisable to hold the nose tightly and pull back on the head so as not to let it become loose; when this happens repeatedly often enough that can cause damage to your head
E semblantment fa quan es pausada sobre le fetge e la melsa deves ventositat en aquels enclausa.	 Similarly placed when you are placed over the belly button and the belly will expand in these small spaces
E aquestas ventozas so administradas vuedas amb succio tant solament; e alcunas veguadas so administradas am foc.	 These openings are administered with suction only, while others are treated by fire.
E alcunas veguadas so administradas plenas de aygua tebeza en las malautias de la melsa.	 Some of these openings are filled with water droplets in the belly button's folds.
E aquo es per que la ventoza sia umplida e sia pus gran, so es aygua cauda sola o aygua en la qual sian cuytas herbas ad aquo convenientz.	 This is done to fill it and keep it full, whether water alone or a mixture of herbs suited for this purpose.
Forma de ventoza aministrada am foc: sia la amplitud del orrifici de dos ditz, segon que nos la havem formada; e la quantitat del preon sia la maytat de un palm; e sia en lo latz de lu, en le loc que es en le circuit, la maytat de lu, le trauc sia petit segon la quantitat que intre en lu una agulha.	 The size of the orifice is determined as follows: two fingers wide when formed, and the amount of urine to be measured with a pipette; and its length in relation to itself, or its circumference, by measuring it at one end against another.
Sia fayta de eram rog o citri, de grosses marges, leon, enguals e terses per so que no leda le membre deves la sua posicio sobre lu.	 The edge of the blade should be placed large enough to prevent the member from slipping off it.
E sia al mieg de lu vergua transversa de eram o de ferr, on es pausada candela am lo foc.	 It can either cross vertically or horizontally at right angles.
E ja sia aquesta ventoza gran major de aquela la qual havem recomtat; e la pauca mendre de aquela segon las malautias e la etat de aquel que usa de aquela.	 The larger the better, unless it is used for a small area like belly button or thighs, and only when they are not injured, should be very gentle.
E las ventosas dels efantz e extenuatz so autres que las ventozas dels joves e de grosses corssas.	 The openings of the fingers and thumbs differ from those of the smaller toes and larger buttocks.
E la qualitat de pausar aquesta ventoza am foc sobre le membre es que extenda la meca am foc de lenha decentment denant una pauca candela de cera, e pausa aquela sobre le mieg de la vergua transversa en le mieg loc de la ventoza, per que le foc sia accendut enviro la partida dejos per que no sia comburit le cors del malaute.	 The quality of the cushion to be placed over a member is that it extends the flame from kindling gently with just a small candle, and pause it on top of the transverse ribcage in place of the cushion, so as not to burn the patient's chest
E aprop sia pausada sobre le membre del malaute, e le dit sia sobre le trauc que havem dit, entro que quan tenem las ventozas e non indigem que osten le dit e que yesca la vapor sobre aquel trauc, lahoras la ventoza sira tantost dissolvuda.	 The cushion is placed over the patient's member and it is put on top of the ribcage where we have told you to place it, so that when you open up the wounds, do not say anything else but what has already been said and let vapor fall onto that ribcage, then the wound will dissolve itself.
E prop igneys la meca segon la sua manieyra, e itera aquela si indigeyssas de aquela.	 Place your hand on top of the body after removing the cushion.
Mays en ventosa que es aministrada en la malautia de plauressi, am aygua, en la qual no ha vergua transversa ni trauc, e no es aministrada sino que sia umplida de aygua, e es pausada sobre le membre tant solament. E aquesta es la forma de lu: E aquesta ventoza quant plus es gran, tant es milhor, per que puya recebre gran quantitat de aygua.	 The method of administering the wound is this way: When it becomes larger in size, so much better, as a large amount of water will be received.

O, filh, sapiatz que jactan se de aquest capitol les fols metges e les vulguars e aquels que degun temps no reguardero les libres dels Antics ni legiro de aquels una letra.	 Oh son, hear that the chapters on medicine are for doctors and pharmacists who use drugs in ancient times

E yeu ja he de aquo descrit en aquest capitol tot aquo que conte la mieua sciencia e sobre le qual es passat lo mieu experiment; pus que agui abreujat aquo a vos autres e deliuregui aquo de occupacio de elonguacio; e abreujegui aquo en la fi de abreujacio; et e monstrat aquo en la fi de declaracio; e formegui en aquo motas formas dels sturmentz que so administratz en aquel, cum es fayt per addicio de declaracio, ayssi cum he fayt en dos capitols precedentz. Capitol primier.	 The First Physician
Summae et collectiones ex esse fracturae ossium, ex eis quarum praemissio necessaria est, antequam incipiamus rememorationem membrorum fraftorum et diversorum si uniuscuiusque. De restauracio de fractura del bras.	 Treatment of a broken arm.

De curacio dels osses trincatz quan so restauratz tortuozament e prohibeys la operacio de lor de aquo que cove.	 "When bones are broken and it is necessary to restore them, they must be forbidden from undergoing further operations of that kind.
Quan accideys al membre ja restaurat aprop la sanacio de lu de tortuositat e eminencia al os trincat e nodacio, e es per aquo fededa de forma del membre, mays empero le membre no es prohibit de la sieua operacio natural, lahora no cove que tu recipias la paraula de aquel que exsistima aquel membre sia de novel trincat.	 "When a member has already been restored to health from its injury and strength returned to the broken bone, it is allowed for that member to undergo its normal operation. However, one must not allow another member of an entirely new broken bone.
Mays ja so statz motz fols metges e restauradors les quals han fayt aquo en nostra tera; e aquesta operacio es mot vituperable perduzent a gran temor le senhal de la qual es mortal.	 "The physicians and restorers who have done this in our time, may their practice be cursed with great fear of that kind which is fatal.
Mays si claudicacio e nodacio son recentz, lahoras cove que sian enbrocatz am aygua tebeza en la qual so coytas erbas mollificantz, ayssi cum son fuelas de altea e razitz de lu, e mellilot, e semblantz ad aquels; e sia fayt a lu emplastre am emplastre mollificatio ayssi cum dyallaquilon ben fayt; o que sia preza mucillage de razit de altea e sia contucida am gray de gualina o am oli de cirami, e sia emplastrat am aquel; o que sian prezes figuas grassas e sian trissadas am fems de colom, e semblantz ad aquels de las medicinas que son nompnadas amermans consolidacio.	 "When recent claudication or nodication occurs, it is customary to bind the affected member with a damp towel in order to soften and soothe them gently; as well as apply warmth from above and below, and also have those placed on their belly and chest respectively; and put it on that place too.
E alcunas vetz es dissolvuda am assidua fricacio leugiera que sia am las mas humidas, e sia administrat movement del membre a tota partida en totas horas.	 Some veins are dissolved by cold fluids that run through the most humid parts of the body and move throughout it during all hours.
Mays si tortuositat ja es anada denant e es fayta fort e convertida es en peyra e provocada es necessitat a curacio de lu am ferr, lahoras cove que sia le pus desus cecsat e la continuacio del os sia dissolvut, e sia inscidit aquo que superflueys de nodacio de aquel meteys am le os am inscissoris subtils, e sia aministrada facilitat en aquel am sollicitut e studi.	 The tortuous veins become enlarged and converted into ulcers when necessary care is not taken to treat them promptly. They are dissolved if the ulcer is not treated, and they may be accompanied by a discharge of fine matter from subtle pores, causing discomfort in that area.
Capitol .xxiii.	 The [section/chapter] thirty-three (33)
De sermo en dislocacio.	 This is the beginning of a sermon on dislocation.
Dislocacio es eyssiment de alcuna de las juncturas del sieu loc, per que es prohibida de movement, e es orrezada la figura del membre, e fa venir sobre le malaute dolors e lesios grans.	 Dislocation is the destruction of some of the joints in that location so as to prevent motion, causing a lump on the member and bringing about great pains and injuries.
Donc quan accideys ad alcu dislocacio, lahoras cove tantost perforsar que sia reduzit, e no tarde aquela reduzir, quar si es tardada, le loc es apostemat e fort leu am aquo es fayta dificil la reduccio de dislocaccio.	 Therefore when dislocation occurs, doctors must make every effort to reduce it as soon as possible and not let time pass by without reducing the dislocation lest it be difficult later on for that reduction of dislocation to occur.
E per aysso no cove que sia maugut ni stendut en la hora de la apostemacio, quar motas veguadas fa venir spasme e dolors ledentz.	 And thus do not let it be that the reduction is done in haste and without care lest spasms and pains follow.
Mays quan aquo accideys, lahoras cove que tu te coytes a la flaubotomia del malaute, e aprop sia layssat entro que repause le apostema; e aprop le membre sia embrocat am aygua cauda e oli, e aprop sia reduzit am facilitat.	 When that occurs, doctors should apply to the patient a cure for gout, and also place something moist between their legs to keep them moist, and also reduce it with ease.
E tot membre sia curat am aquo del qual la rememoracio vindra en son loc.	 When each part of the body has been infiltrated by cold humors causing joint pain, especially in the feet, it is commonly known as gout among doctors
E yeu ja e ordenatz les capitols de dislocacio segon que es precedit en fractura; de la partida del cos pus sobirana entro a la partida pus dejos.	 You already opened up space between the patient's thighs, placed cushions underneath them, another servant on their legs and another on their chest holding onto their hands.
Capitol .xxiiii.	 The twelfth chapter.
De curacio de dislocacio de la mandibula dejos.	 Care for dislocation of the mandible (lower jaw).
So dislocadas las doas mandibulas si no tart; e la dislocacio de amdos es fayta segon una de dos manieyras: que o son remaugudas de lurs locs per pauca remocio, e so mollificadas un petit; o so dislocadas per entiera dislocacio e complida, entro que sian mollificadas a la partida de la junctura entro que corro saliva del malaute e que no puesca tenir aquela ni puesca claure la sua boca, e la lengua de lu sia envolopada en sa paraula.	 If the lower jaw is dislocated and cannot be returned to its place with a slight force or by removing a small part of it, then it must be separated further so that saliva does not come out; if after separation from the mouth, tongue must still be covered inside the mouth.
Mays quan la dislocacio de lu es pauca, lahoras en las majors disposicios retorna per si an pauca causa.	 When dislocation is slight, doctors return to their original position with a small force.
Mays si la dislocacio es entiera e complida, lahoras cove que sia administrada reduccio de lu leugierament, e no sia tardada de tot.	 If the dislocation is complete and complicated, then it must be reduced immediately by skilled surgeons who will not wait for too long
E es que·l ministre tengua le cap del malaute, e entrometa lo metge le dit pous de la una sieua ma en la razit de la dislocacio de la mandibula dedintz la boca de lu, si la dislocacio es de la una part; o que entrometa les sieus dos pouzes ensemps, si la dislocacio es de doas partz, e les autres ditz de las mas de lu sian defora am les quals enguale; e comanda al malaute que cesse las suas mandibulas e absolva aquelas anar de quascuna partida; e le metge engualhe la mandibula e enpellisca la mandibula entro que retorne al sieu loc.	 The minister holds the patient's head, and the surgeon puts their thumb in the mouth to control it if there is only one dislocation or both thumbs inside as long as they are able to hold them properly; then the surgeon places the mandible back into its place.
E si dificil es la reducio de lu, e majorment si amdos las mandibulas so essemps dislocadas, lahoras aministra evoporacio am aygua cauda e oli, entro que sia fayta leugiera la reduccio de amdos e no tardes la reduccio de amdos de tot, ayssi quo havem dit.	 When it is difficult to reduce them, and especially if the jaws are very loose or dislocated, the doctor will administer a solution of water and oil into their mouth, so that they can swallow the reduction easily without difficulty
E donc cum retornam e so engualadas, e es clausa la boca del malaute e no es mollificada, lahoras pausa sobre aquelas polvils de drap am cerot, e sia fayt de cera e oli rozat; e aprop sia liat am facilitat am liamens mols.	 Once the jaws are returned and aligned as much as possible, do not open the patient's mouth too wide, the doctor will put a cloth soaked with oil onto them to facilitate swallowing the reduction gently.
E sia le dormir del malaute sobre le sieu dos, e·l cap de lu sia stant entre dos aurelhes, per so que no maugue aquel a la partida dreyta ni a la sinistra; e no li fassas per forsa masteguar alcuna causa; habans la sieua vianda sia forbicio leon, entro que quan las dolors sian remaugudas e las mandibulas so nozadas, lahoras maugue aquo que vol.	 The patient should lie on their back with the head between two pillows to ensure that they cannot move suddenly or to one side without being guided; have a pillow placed under their chin as well, for comfort and support.
E aquo sia aministrat am facilita, e no trebalhe sobre la apercio de la boca deves la comestio e beure e ocitatio, entro que la mandibula sia nozada e sanada.	 This is when it has been administered easily and the jaws are in good condition.
E si es dificil la reduccio de duas mandibulas quan so dislocadas en alcuna hora e no so convertidas als lors locs, lahoras motas veguadas accideysso febres e soda assidua, e fort leu es alerguat le ventre del malaute, e fort leu e vomeys colera pura.	 If the reduction of both jaws is difficult when they are dislocated at any time and not converted to their correct position, doctors will administer a purge with hot water, salt water, and vinegar, as well as heat pads for belly, as well as heating pad for coldness and vomiting.
E quan tu vezes aquo, lahoras sapias que es perdicio; e motas veguadas mor aquel al qual accideys aquo en x dias.	 When you do this, the doctor will tell you that they have lost it; and if you are experiencing this for more than two days in a row, then you should consult with another doctor.
Capitol .xxv.	 "When pain arises from cold humors infiltrating each part of the body, as when it occurs in the feet.
De reduccio de la dislocacio de la furcula e de la extremitat del muscle.	 Translation: To reduce or prevent dislocation of the shoulder blade and extremity of the muscle.
Furcula no es dislocada del latz dedintz per la sua continuacio am le pietz; e alcunas veguadas es dislocada a la partida defora, e aquo es declarat al sentiment.	 Translation: The furcula does not dislocate from below due to its continuous contact with the chest; and some vertebrae are dislocated at the start of the process, which is known as the feeling of being lifted up
E la restauracio de lu es que·l malaute jagua sobre le sieu dos e extenda les sieus brasses.	 Translation: The restoration or healing of it involves placing the patient on their back and extending their limbs.
E aprop coarta le loc am la tua palma am fort coartacio, quar ela retornara.	 Translation: And if you tightly hold down the area with a strong grasp so that it returns.
E aprop pausa sobre aquela emplastre e pulvils e strenh aquela.	 Translation: Then place your hand over this surface and dust, and firmly press it down.
Mays la extremitat de aquel que siec le coyde e·s continuat am aquel, no es dislocada en alcun dia; lahoras cove que sia reduzida e engualhada segon que havem dit e segon que es a tu aparelhat.	 Translation: When the extremity has been cut open and continues with it without dislocation occurring on any day, then the pain is reduced or prevented from happening as you mentioned earlier and secondly when you hold down their hand.
E aprop pausa sobre aquela emplastre, e pulvils, e extrictura, e comanda al malaute adherir a trenquilitat e a repaus entro que sia sanat.	 Translation: Then place your hand over this surface and dust; press it firmly down and command the patient to adhere to tranquility and rest so that they feel well.
E am aquesta meteyssa curacio es reduzida la extremita del muscle quan es separada del sieu loc.	 Translation: The reduction in the pain of the muscle extremity occurs when it is separated from its location
Capitol .xxvi.	 "When the pain arises from excessive heat, as when it occurs in the feet.
De la reduccio de la dislocacio del muscle.	 Translation: To reduce or prevent dislocation of the muscle.
Sapias que·l muscle no es dislocat sino segon tres manieras, de las quals es la una que sia dislocat a la partida del titillic a la partida dejos.	 The first sentence translates to "The muscle is not dislocated but rather in three ways, one of which it may be dislocated at the beginning/start of the thread and another at the end.
E la segonda es que sia dislocat a la partida desus del muscle, e aquo es fayt tart; e no es dislocat a las partidas detras per la spalla; e no es dislocat a las partidas denant per les nervis.	 The second sentence translates to "And the second is that it may be dislocated at the start of the muscle, and this occurs frequently; but it is not dislocated at the back part by the shoulder; nor is it dislocated in front parts through nerves.
E majorment es dislocat e defora eyssit a las partidas dejos deves le titillic, e majorment en aquels dels quals las carns son paucas, leugierament es dislocat; mays en aquels en les quals so motas carns, es eyssit fora am dificultat.	 The last sentence translates to "And most of all it is dislocated at the start parts of the thread, and frequently occurs in those where there are few veins; however, when it happens in those where the fat cells are present, then it is very difficult.
E fort leu accideys ad alcus homes percussio o cazement, e le muscle de lu es apostemat de apostema caut, e es cujat per aquo que ja sia dislocat.	 The last sentence translates to "In the unfortunate case of a sudden impact or collision that is made directly on it, and if this has been dislocated then immediately tighten/clamp it.
Adonc cove que tu sproes aquo entro que estias sobre-sertetut de lu, e lahoras procesiscas en la curacio de lu.	 The last sentence translates to "And now that you are on top of the treatment for him/her, proceed in the care of them.
E es conoguda la dislocacio de lu quan es a las partidas dejos deves le titillic; per so que distingescas entre le muscle dislocat e·l muscle sa, quar tu atrobas entre aquels diversitat manifesta; e atrobas en le cap del muscle concavitat e dejos le titillic deves le tocament del cap del muscle ayssi quo un huou, e al malaute no pot redusir la sua ma a la sieua aurelha, ni maure aquela per totz movementz.	 The last sentence translates to "You can distinguish between the dislocated muscle and the normal one by feeling for these various manifestations; you place your finger in the head of the concave muscle at which point it must touch the chest hair below, so that a hand cannot reduce its size or stretch over all movements.
Si es dislocat deves le pietz o ensus, e tu lahoras atrobas manifest tocament, e no es amaguat.	 When joints are dislocated, place a cushion on them, and the pains will subside immediately, without any delay.
E de aquesta dislocacio es fayta leugiera reduccio quan es fresca e le malaute es enfant.	 The dislocation should be reduced as quickly as possible when it is fresh and the patient is young.
E la reduccio de lu es que·l ministre eleva la ma de lu a las partidas desus; e aprop pause les tieus pouses dejos le titillic de lu, e eleva la junctura am fortaleza en sus al sieu loc, e·l ministre eleva la ma de lu, e extenda aquela en sus; e aprop pausa aquela dejos quar ela retorna leugierament.	 The reduction is done by placing the hand of the patient on their chest, and holding them tightly with both hands while extending it above where it should be placed, the minister places his hand over it as well to prevent its return.
Mays si per aquo que havem dit no retorna, e so del comensament que accidic la dislocacio, motz dias, lahoras cove que·l malaute sia banhat en aygua cauda e sia aministrada enbrocacio que mollifique e liniesca ayssi cum si so coytz razitz de altea, e fenugrec, e melillot en aygua, e sia administrada.	 If what has been said does not return or if it is the beginning of a dislocation, then days should be avoided, and pain must be administered by breaking up with cold water, soothing and linifying so that cuts may heal quickly, making them smooth, while avoiding cuts from swelling, softening and melting in water.
E aprop le malaute sia ressupinat sobre le sieu dos e sia pausat dejos le titillic de lu espera de lana que sia engual entre levitat e strictura, e aprop le metge pause le sieu talo sobre la spera, e eleva le cap del muscle am vertut, e atire la ma del malaute per que no sia mauguda a las partidas dejos, e autre ministre tengua le cap del malaute, que no sia maugut a las partidas dejos, quar aquela tantost retorna al sieu loc.	 The patient is placed on their back with their feet elevated and the doctor holds their head in order to prevent it from falling while also lifting up their arm above where they want the joint reduced or stretched out.
E si voles, reduzeys aquel segon aquesta manieyra: e es que tu fassas esser prezent un home le qual sia pus lonc que·l malaute, e estia de la part de aquel latz, e entrometa le sieu muscle dejos le titillic del malaute e eleve le titillic de lu a las partidas desus entro que·l malaute sia suspendut en ayre, e autre ministre tire la ma del malaute de las partidas dejos del sieu ventre.	 If you want to reduce that joint with another method: and it is necessary for the patient's spouse to enter from the side of his buttocks into their abdomen, where they place a finger over the affected joint of the patient while supporting them above in order to hold the joint down.
Mays si le malaute es leugier, lahoras cove que am lu que autre causa sia suspenduda, per so que grave aquel, quar la dislocacio retorna tantost.	 When a patient lies down, pain occurs between their thighs, therefore holding it tightly prevents further dislocation of the joint.
E es reduzit eysament segon autra manieyra: e es que sia ficat en terra un fust lonc le cap del qual sia redon de figura, ayssi cum pilo de mortier, que no sia gros ni subtil, e aprop sia pausat dejos le malaute; pus que so pausatz sobre·l cap del fust draps leons, e·l malaute sia stant segon la longitut del fust, e aprop sia extenduda la ma de lu a las partidas dejos del autra part; e sia extendut le cos de lu del autre part am fortaleza, quar la junctura retorna al sieu loc am velocitat.	 Another way to reduce pain is by placing the patient's head on a cushion of appropriate size and shape, such as one with a pillow placed underneath it to prevent suffocation, so that their legs are positioned over it; then extend both arms from the other part of the body towards where the joint should return.
E si es dificil reduccio de lu per totas las causas que havem ditas, lahoras usa de aquesta cura: e es que tu prenguas un fust la quantitat del qual sia en le lonc de dos brasses, e latitut de aquel sia de quatre ditz, e la grossetut de lu sia aleujat en le preon del tittilic segon aquesta forma:	 If it is difficult to reduce pain due to all the causes mentioned earlier, then doctors use this treatment: and take a cushion that has a length of two fists (approximately 14 inches or about half a meter), and its height should be four times as long.
E aprop sobre le cap redon sian liatz drap leons per so que·l fust no ledesca le malaute.	 Make sure the cushion covers their head to prevent it from slipping off.
E aprop sia pausat dejos le titillic del malaute, e sia extenduda la ma o le bras sobre·l fust entro a las partidas dejos, e sia liat le fust sobre le adjutori e le bras e la extremitat de la ma.	 Then place the cushion over their chest and put one arm on top of it to rest both arms there, covering the area between them with another hand or finger placed at its edge as well.
Aprop sia pausat le bras sobre un scalo de scala segon la latitut, e la ma sia extenduda a las partidas dejos, e l’autre cos sia suspendut de l’autre part, quar la junctura intra tantost.	 Then place both arms on top of each other at the height specified and put one arm or finger between them as well to hold it in place securely.
E cum le intrament de lu es complit segon quascuna maniera que es a tu possibla, e lahoras cove que tu pauses dejos le titillic spera de lana de engual quantitat; e aprop pauza emplastre perparat de polvera de moli am enses e album de huou sobre tot le muscle, ayssi quo es revolvut desus, e aprop strenh dejos le titillic am strictura decent; e le liament sia revolvut sobre le emplastre, e la ma de lu sia annectida al col de lu, e sia leyssat, e no sia mauguda la ma de lu per vii dias.	 The first sentence translates to: With the complete disintegration of each one in every possible manner that suits you, and after pausing, place a pillow over them as much as you want; and prepare for preventing from the pole of molly from this, and also the album on top of everything muscle, so it will be revolved by them, and tie up the leg of him to the column of him, and leave it, but not to hurt the leg of him per seven days.
E cove que sia pausada la vianda del malaute pauca, entro que·l membre sia confortat, quar es pus leugier a la sanacio de lu.	 After pausing briefly with the member of patient in comfort, once it is healed, you will guide him to the treatment of his illness.
E aprop la vianda sia donada major aprop vii o v e sia exercitat un movement; e donc si es fermat e no es mollificat, lahoras ja es sanat.	 Give the bandage a big one or two, and exercise it with some movements; if it is tight but not loose, then doctors have already done so
Mays si la junctura es dislocada motas veguadas per humiditat que accideys a lu o per autra causa, lahoras cove que en aquela sia administrat cauteri am tres traucs, segon que denant es dit en le capitol de cauteri.	 If the joint is dislocated due to heat or another cause, then it should be treated with three cuts, after which a dressing of cautery will be applied in its capital
E si tot aysso es fayt e aprop vii dias es desliat le liament e la junctura no es fermada, e le emplastre e la strictura son reduzitz sobre lu alcunas veguadas, e no es fermada e catz e no pot elevar aquel bras a las partidas desus, lahoras sapias que·ls nervis de lu, les quals so al cap del muscle, ja so inscizes o extendutz o mollificatz, e sapia que la junctura nul temps no sira ficada en loc sieu.	 If all this is done and the joint and ligament are not tight, then loose them gradually over time, do not tighten it too much or make it tight; otherwise, you will know that the nerves of him, which are at the top of the muscle, will be injured, crushed or elongated, and may not be fixed in place.
De la dislocacio de aquela qu’es fayta deves le pietz e la mamilha o las partidas detras, la reduccio es fayta am impulcio e extencio am las mas, entro que retorne.	 "From the dislocation of that which you have spread open to release the bowels and buttocks or behind the legs, reduction is necessary with a swift impulse so that it returns.
E sia administrada en aquela l’autra strictura, e cura aquela entro que sia sanada.	 "Then apply ointment on the other restriction, and cure this one to be healed.
E si accideys aprop la sanacio gravitat en le membre e tarditat en le movement de lu, lahoras le malaute uze de banh motas veguadas entro que aquela gravitat sia alleujada e que retorne a la natura de lu primiera.	 "And if you see the swelling of the member and delay in its movement, then apply lotion to reduce swelling and restore back to normal.
Capitol .xxvii.	 This is likely referring to Chapter 27 of a larger work.
De curacio de dislocacio del coyde.	 "For the treatment of dislocation.
Sapias que la junctura del coyde es dislocada am difficultat e semblantment retorna am difficultat; e aquela es dislocada a totas partidas, e majorment a la partida denant a la partida detras, e la dislocacio de lu no es amaguada a tu quar es cazent dejos le vezement o dejos le tocament segon qualque figura sia dislocat, e quan ajustes le coyde disloguat am le sa, aquo es a tu declarat manifestament, quar la junctura es concavada e no pot doblar le bras, ni tocar am aquel le sieu muscle.	 "The joint of the thigh is dislocated with great difficulty and returns to greater difficulty; when it is dislocated on both sides, mostly at the front side as behind, and its dislocation cannot be healed by touch or movement because this joint is concave and cannot bend the arms, nor touch against that muscle.
E cove que·t coytes, e reduzescas la dislocacio tantost denant que vengua a lu apostema caut, quar si ve a lu apostema caut, dificil es la reduccio de lu, e fort leu no es sanat de tot; e majorment quan es a las partidas detras, quar pus mala es de totas las autras specias de dislocacio, e de major dolor, e motas veguadas deyssen am aquela la mort.	 "And you say that the dislocation must be reduced as soon as possible to prevent further complications such as burns and frostbite; when it is a cauterized dislocation, if there are, difficult reduction of the joint occurs, and great pain occurs with all other types of dislocations, and many cases death.
E la restauracio de lu, quan es aquela que es possibla reduzir, es que la ma de lu sia extenduda am doas mas, e le bras de lu sia expandut, e las mas del metge sian sobre le coyde e dejos lu, e el empellisca la junctura am les pouzes de las suas mas ensemps, o am la razit de la sua palma entro que torne en son loc.	 When the restoration is possible to reduce it, extend the leg with both legs wide apart and expand your arms, so that the surgeon can see clearly inside the joints or the palm of his hand before turning back into place
Mays si la dislocacio es a las partidas denant, lahoras retorna ayssi que dobla la ma am la sua ma, entro que percuta le coyde am la razit de la sua palma.	 When dislocation occurs on the parts of the day and night, then return to double spread your arms as wide as possible inside so that you can cut into the palm area
E si la dislocacio no obezeys a la reduccio, lahoras aministra vehement extencio e mot fort.	 If dislocation cannot be reduced at all, then administer violent stretching and strong massage.
E es que dos ministres extendan le bras, e tenguan aquel eyssament dos ministres per so que no sia remaugut deves la extencio.	 And two servants extend your arms as wide as possible to prevent you from being stretched out.
E aprop sia revolvut le bras deves tota part, pus que es envolopat drap doblat lonc sobre la ma de lu, o liament.	 Then return your arms to their full range of motion, and place a folded blanket on the leg as well.
E quant le metge toca la junctura am la sua ma, unte aquela am alcun oli per so que aquo sia aquelas causas las quals ajudan en lubricitat de la junctura am facilitat; e aprop empellesca la junctura am empulcio vehement entro que retorne.	 When the surgeon touches your hand at the joint, then apply something to make it slippery and easy for him/her to move around inside that joint quickly and return it back in place.
E aprop la reduccio de lu cove que sia pausat sobre aquela empastre en le qual sia stipticitat e excequacio am album de huou, e sia extrenhut am strictura descent, e·l bras sia suspendut del col, e sia layssat per alcus dias.	 Then place the reduction on a cushion which has stiffness and looseness, stretch it with firm pressure, and hold your arm at an angle for some time.
E aprop sia desliat; e donc si la junctura es formada en le sieu loc, lahoras tu deslia le liament de lu e layssa aquela.	 When a joint is formed in that place, doctors remove the ligament of it and arrange it like this
E si vezas la junctura no be strenher, lahoras tu itera le emplastre e·l liament, e layssa aquela per alcus dias entro que sia extrenhuda; e aprop deslia aquela.	 If the joint is not too stiff, doctors put the splint and ligament together again, arranging them so that they are together for several days until it hardens
Mays si accideys a lu gravitat aprop la reduccio de la junctura, e la disposicio de lu es en movement, lahoras aministra humectacio en banh e fricacio subtil, e comprecio, entro que sia aleujat; o pausa sobre la junctura aleliati, so es coyssa de moto grassa; e aprop sia liada, e layssa aquela sobre le os le dia e la nueyt.	 If the joint is unstable and mobility is reduced, doctors administer a humectant (a substance that holds water) and lubricant (subtle friction reducer), so that it becomes loose again; or to pause the joint from excessive motion with a splint, as may be necessary; and arrange it in such a way that it can move freely when needed.
E aprop osta aquela, e met aquel en banh; e quan suza, lahoras tu fregua la junctura am fricacio temprada, e aprop itera sobre aquela aleliati, so es ronhonal de moto, una veguada, e la segonda, e la .iii.a.,	 Then apply the splint on top of that, and when you put it back in place, doctors will gently rub or apply a lubricant to the joint again to make sure there is no excessive friction, ensuring free motion one by one.
