E cove que sia aministrada compressio am taula sobre le loc al qual yeys la junctura.	 Doctors administer compression therapy over the affected joint.
Donc cum la reducio es complida segon que cove — e·l senhal de la reduccio de lu no es amaguat a tu, e es que tu extendas del malaute doas cambas, e quan tu vezes aquelas enguals e le malaute extrenh la sieua camba e expandeys aquela ses excusacio, lahoras sapias que·l membre segon que cove es retornat — e lahoras tu ajusta doas coyssas e pausa empastre e extrenh am benda ayssi que la ancha no sia mauguda en alcuna de las partidas; e adheresca le malaute a repaus per tres dias o per quatre.	 Once the reduction is complete, ensure that both legs are extended and apply pressure to the affected joint with the heel of one hand. Then gently press down on the other thigh as well. If you notice any excoriation or pain during this process, doctors recommend placing a cushion between your fingers while applying pressure to prevent injury.
E aprop deslia le liament e l’empastre, e compara la una camba am l’autra.	 Ensure that both legs are extended and press down on the affected joint with one hand.
Lahoras, si vezas aquelas enguals en vustament, lahoras sapias que la dislocacio ja es fermada, e adonc layssa le malaute anar.	 Joints become inflamed when there is a blockage in circulation to them.
E si vezas alcuna causa de mollificacio, lahoras tu retorna e emplastra aquel, e extrenh aquel segon la tua primiera strectura, e layssa aquel en tres dias.	 If no cause of pain relief is found, the physician will return and retest after three days.
E aprop deslia aquel, e fay aquel tardar en ambulacio sobre quascu per alcus dias, entro que sia confortat.	 And then apply this remedy, taking care to do it quickly before any blisters occur, until the pain is relieved and comfort is felt.
Capitol .xxxii.	 Chapter 32 of a book?
De curacio de dislocacio del denolh.	 Treatment for joint inflammation.
Le denolh es dislocat segon tres manieyras, quar es dislocat a las partidas defora, e a las partidas dedintz, e a las partidas dejos mays a las partidas detras; e a las partidas denant no es dislocat.	 Joint dislocation is corrected after three months at the front, back and below, but not in front of the belly button.
E le senhal de dislocacio de lu es que comandes al malaute que aplique la sua camba am la coyssa; lahoras sapias que·l denol es dislocat.	 The treatment for dislocation is that you command the patient to apply his cushion on top of the thigh, and it will be corrected by him.
E la restauracio de totas las manieyras de lu es que fassas cezer le malaute dreyt, enayssi que ja extenda la sieua camba, si pot sobre aquo; adherir le tieu dos a la cara de lu, e pausa le pe de lu entre les tieus pes; e aprop fay adherir le denol de lu am las tuas palmas, e rete aquelas entre les tieus ditz sobre le denolh de lu am fortaleza, e autre ministre extenda le sieu pe entro que·l denol retorne a son loc.	 The restoration of all the fingers is to make the patient put his hands on top, and then extend his cushion if able; hold two fingers in front of him, place one finger between each thumb and pointer finger of his hand; and then apply his hand over the dislocation holding it firmly until it returns to its place.
E senhal de reddicio de lu es que la sua camba adharesca am la coyssa am levitat no-laboroza.	 The abdomen of the patient will be opened up, allowing the surgeon to see inside.
E aprop emplastra aquel e fay adhirir la camba am la coyssa, e aprop lia aquelas emsemps am una benda per tres dias o per quatre, e aprop deslia aquelas.	 The servant is placed between the thighs of the patient and stays in place for three or four days depending on the situation, then removed.
E no uze le malaute de ambulacio per alcus dias, entro que sia sanat e cofortat.	 The patient will be taken care of during their stay until they are healed and comfortable
Mays si la reduccio de lu a tu es excusada, lahoras aministra fort extencio am liamentz dels quals en la curacio de la hancha precedit narracio.	 If the reduction is excused, it means that the surgeon will provide extensive care during the recovery period from previous surgery.
Capitol .xxxiii.	 The end of this text
De la curacio de la dislocacio del talo.	 And for the treatment and healing of the dislocation
Le talo alcunas veguadas es remaugut per petita remocio, e alcunas veguadas es dislocat segon compliment, e la dislocacio de lu es fayta o a las partidas dedintz o a las partidas deforo.	 The toes are bent and straightened once more, and the dislocation of it will be done by hand or with forceps.
E le senhal de la dislocacio de lu es que vezes le talo imflat procedent a la partida a la qual es dislocat.	 It means that after the dislocation is made, the toes should straighten naturally to their previous position.
Mays la curacio de la remocio de lu es de leugiera reddicio, e es que sia extendut am facilitat am las mas e sia engualhat entro que retorne.	 The treatment for straightening of the leg is by using a straightener device, and it should be used as easily as possible until it returns to its original position.
Mays en la curacio de lu quan es dislocat segon compliment, cove que fasses cezer le malaute dreyt, e tengua aquel un ministre fort e valent de la partida detras del dos de aquel en le mieg loc de lu.	 When a dislocation occurs for the second time after straightening it, you should make sure to pull gently on the patient's arm behind them and keep applying force until the leg returns into place.
E aprop te tu am la tieua ma dreyta le pe de la pus sobirana part, e am la tua ma sinistra de la part pus dejos del pe en le loc de la cavilha.	 The first sentence translates to "Here you place your right hand on the lower part of the thigh and left hand on the upper part of the foot in the hollow below.
E aprop atira le pe a tu am la tua ma dreyta, e aprop am la sinistra per dos veguadas, e aprop exten am la sinistra; e empelleys le pietz del pe am la dreyta deves la camba ses trebalh.	 The sentence is describing the correct positioning for performing a cautery procedure on the foot. Here's how it translates: "Place your right hand in front of your left hand, and put both hands over the hollow below to support them.
E fay aquo doas veguadas segon que havem comtat.	 The sentence implies that this is just a step taken after performing other procedures or actions related to the patient's condition.
E aprop empelleys le pietz del pe a la camba la tersa veguada, e tu es a la cavilha.	 This final sentence suggests that once you have performed the cautery procedure on one part of the foot (the lower part), proceed to perform it on the other part (upper part).
Donc si retorna en una veguada o en dos segon aquesta manieyra, e si vezes le pe engualhat, es bo; e sino, lahoras sobre lu itera la operacio, quar aquel retorna.	 This sentence implies that if the procedure is performed in one or two steps as described earlier and you successfully perform both procedures then everything will be fine. However, if things go wrong during either of them, doctors should intervene to correct this issue.
Mays si a tu es prohibida la reduccio de lu am aquo que havem recomtat, lahoras fay jaser le malaute sobre le sieu dos sobre terra, e estrenh un paysel mot en terra fermat, e que caja entre las coyssas de lu, e tu ja has envolopat sobre lu drap per so que no ledesca le malaute.	 This sentence means that if the recommended reduction method is prohibited and doctors should proceed as follows: lay the patient on their back with a pillow placed firmly on the ground between their thighs, cover them completely with a blanket to prevent the hernia from slipping out of place.
E aprop le ministre de lu tengua las suas coyssas, e aprop autre ministre extenda le pe am las suas mas o am liament que lie sobre le col del pe; e aprop extenda aquel quascun ministre contre extencio del sieu par, e le payssel sia extant entre las coyssas del malaute retinent aquel, per so que·l cos de lu no sia atirat a las partidas dejos deves la sua extencio.	 The sentence suggests that after placing the patient on their back with the pillow placed below them between their thighs and covering them completely with a blanket to prevent the hernia from slipping out of place, another servant should extend one hand onto their waist or side while keeping the other hand extended against the chest as it is held by the first servant. This ensures that nothing protrudes outside so everything remains contained within the cavity below.
E aprop le metge enguala la dislocacio am las sieuas mas, e autre ministre tengua la coyssa sana a las partidas dejos, quar la dislocacio retorna am la facilitat.	 When the doctor makes an incision on your breast or leg, another attendant should hold the healthy shoulder to prevent it from moving around, and another minister should have the cushion in place at all joints of theirs, so that the dislocation returns easily.
E donc cum retorna la dislocacio e es declarada a tu la sanetat de la reduccio de lu, lahoras pausa emplastre e extrenh aquela am liamentz fortment, e ligua le pe am liament a la camba.	 When the dislocation is returned and declared as healed by your doctor, you should remove the splint and stretch that area gently but firmly, and bind it up with tape on the leg above.
E cove que temes o te guardes dels nervis les quals so detras sobre le talo, per que le liament sobre aquel no sia vehement e leda aquel fortment.	 You should take care of any nerves that are behind your heel to prevent them from tightening and causing harm to it.
E aprop layssa aquel per dos dias o per tres; e si le liament es mollificat, extrenh aquel.	 Leave it in place for two or three days if the bandage is loose enough, and if it loosens up you should remove it.
E aprop deslia aquel en le ters dia o en le quart, e prohibeys le malaute de anament per xl dias.	 Remove it on the third day at the latest, or preferably on the fourth, but do not let your patient go without it for more than four days.
Mays si es forsat de anar denant aquel spazi, no es fayta segurtat que la dislocacio no sia sobre lu dissolvuda e corrumpuda, e aprop aquo que no recipia curacio.	 If you want to take it off before the wound has healed and been cured completely, do not be afraid that the dislocation will remain open or infected, but rather prepare for care.
E si accideys a lu apostema caut, lahoras cove que tu aministre en la cedacio de lu aquo en lo qual precedic la nostra narracio, en autre loc de curacio e de embrocacio, entro que sia remauguda.	 If the pointed cautery is used at this stage in healing or anointing, be sure that it precedes our account and goes into other parts of care and anointing until it has healed completely.
Capitol .xxxiiii.	 Conclusion.
De curacio de dislocacio dels ditz dels pes.	 Treatment for foot dislocations.
Cove que aquel qu’es dislocat sia engualhat am pauca extencio ses trebal; e aquo que no es dificil, abantz es leugier.	 When someone's dislocated joint causes very little pain, then it is easy to move around.
Mays si la dislocacio es en alcus nozes del dos del pe, lahoras cove que fassas cezer le malaute le sieu pe sobre loc engual de la terra o sobre taula, e sia estant ayssi cum si anava.	 If the dislocation is on one of your feet, then stretch it gently towards a flat surface or table, being careful not to twist it as you would do otherwise.
E aprop tu sta de pes, e pausa le tieu pe sobre aquo que imineys de las juncturas, e aprop calca aquel am le tieu pe am vertut entro que retorne, e que vejas aquel ja engualhat e no aparesca en le loc eminencia.	 When you are on your stomach and place your foot over the area of the joints, stretch it gently towards a point where it will be straight if straightened out, then return to its original position without making any sound or noise.
E aprop pausa dejos le ventre del pe de lu una taula que prengua tot le pe, a la qual sian dos caps, e aprop strenh aquel am strectura decent e ferma per tres dias; e aprop deslia aquel e fay aquel repausar de ambulacio per motz dias, entro que sia estrenhut e de reddicio sia assegurat.	 When you place your foot on a table with two legs and stretch it gently for three days, then stop stretching when the pain is gone or reduced to the extent that movement becomes difficult, but ensure rest of three days before resuming activity again.
Capitol .xxxv.	 Chapter 55
De las specias de dislocacio que sian faytas am plagua o am fractura o am quascuna ensemps.	 Among the types of dislocations are those that occur in sprains or fractures, as well as any other kind.
Quan accideys alcuna causa de aquelas, e tu te perforssas en la curacio de aquela e en la restauracio de lu, motas veguadas succezeys la mort.	 When a cause of those dislocations occurs and you are unable to treat it or restore its function, that is what leads to death.
E per aquo no cove que sobre la curacio de lu presuma, sino aquel que es savi en l’art, de lonc uzatge, misericordios e pietados, tardiu, no-ardit ni presomptuos; e que use en le comensament de medicinas que cedan apostemas cautz tant solament, e leyssa le malaute al divinal jutgament, sino ad aquel al qual speras salut de perdicio, am de la malautia alleviacio, e en la qual appareys alcuna speransa.	 Therefore, instead of focusing on the healing process itself, it is better to treat the cause and use medicines that give hope only for recovery from disease or injury, rather than giving a cure for death itself, which does not appear possible; with all its consequences
E adonc esforsa te tantost far de lu la reduccio en le comensament de la causa, denant que endevengua apostema caut.	 When you have cut through the flesh of a patient so that the cause is evident from the beginning, then do not hesitate to use the cautery.
E adonc si le membre retorna segon que volem, lahoras aministra regiment le qual ceda apostema caut e cura la plagua am aquo que conveneys a lu dels enguentz desiccatius.	 After removing that member and you want to apply the treatment, then provide the cautery as well as cure for the pain in that area caused by the dry blisters
E si dislocacio es am fractura e accideys en le os satagias separadas, lahoras tu perforsa le stement de lor, e fay en aquo so que havem dit en las malautias simplas de aquo que es precedit en les locz de aquels.	 If dislocation is the fracture and occurs in separate parts of the body, then apply a statement as well to prevent it from spreading further, and make sure you've already done so in the preceding areas.
E guarda e esquiva segon la tua vertut aquel del intrament en las vias de temor segon que a tu es precedida la mia predicacio; quar aquo es milhor a tu deves le tieu Creator, e mays permanent a la tua gloria, e mays saludos al tieu cos verays aquels en le tieu temps.	 Save and avoid second the use of that which is forbidden in the ways of terror lest you may be preceded by my warning; for what I say here is most important to you so that it may last forever, and may greet your body on this day as well as all those after.
Ayssi fineysso las paraulas de Albucasim perfieytament de las quals Dieus ne sia benezeyt.	 And these phrases of Albulcasis are properly translated to the extent that God will be pleased with them.
Amen.	 Amen
